_Scripts2:NewButton('Rejoin', 'Rejoin To Your Current Server', function()
    local _PlaceId = game.PlaceId
    local u32 = {}
    local u33 = ''
    local _hour = os.date('!*t').hour

    if not pcall(function()
        u32 = game:GetService('HttpService'):JSONDecode(readfile('NotSameServers.json'))
    end) then
        table.insert(u32, _hour)
        writefile('NotSameServers.json', game:GetService('HttpService'):JSONEncode(u32))
    end

    function TPReturner()
        local v35

        if u33 ~= '' then
            v35 = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. _PlaceId .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100&cursor=' .. u33))
        else
            v35 = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. _PlaceId .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100'))
        end
        if v35.nextPageCursor and (v35.nextPageCursor ~= 'null' and v35.nextPageCursor ~= nil) then
            u33 = v35.nextPageCursor
        end

        local v36, v37, v38 = pairs(v35.data)
        local v39 = 0

        while true do
            local v40

            v38, v40 = v36(v37, v38)

            if v38 == nil then
                break
            end

            local v41 = true
            local u42 = tostring(v40.id)

            if tonumber(v40.maxPlayers) > tonumber(v40.playing) then
                local v43, v44, v45 = pairs(u32)

                while true do
                    local v46

                    v45, v46 = v43(v44, v45)

                    if v45 == nil then
                        break
                    end
                    if v39 == 0 then
                        if tonumber(_hour) ~= tonumber(v46) then
                            pcall(function()
                                delfile('NotSameServers.json')

                                u32 = {}

                                table.insert(u32, _hour)
                            end)
                        end
                    elseif u42 == tostring(v46) then
                        v41 = false
                    end

                    v39 = v39 + 1
                end

                if v41 == true then
                    table.insert(u32, u42)
                    wait()
                    pcall(function()
                        writefile('NotSameServers.json', game:GetService('HttpService'):JSONEncode(u32))
                        wait()
                        game:GetService('TeleportService'):TeleportToPlaceInstance(_PlaceId, u42, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
                    end)
                    wait(4)
                end
            end
        end
    end
    function Teleport()
        while wait() do
            pcall(function()
                TPReturner()

                if u33 ~= '' then
                    TPReturner()
                end
            end)
        end
    end

    Teleport()
end)
_Scripts2:NewButton('Auto Rejoin', 'Rejoin When Get Kicked/Disconnected', function()
    _Players = game.Players

    game.CoreGui:FindFirstChild('RobloxPromptGui'):FindFirstChild('promptOverlay').DescendantAdded:Connect(function(p47)
        if p47.Name == 'ErrorTitle' then
            p47:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Text'):Connect(function()
                if p47.Text:sub(0, 12) == 'Disconnected' then
                    if #_Players:GetPlayers() > 1 then
                        game:GetService('TeleportService'):TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, game.JobId, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
                    else
                        _Players.LocalPlayer:Kick('Rejoining...')
                        wait()
                        game:GetService('TeleportService'):Teleport(game.PlaceId, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end)
end)

_MyScriptsHaxker_6666666Script:NewDropdown('Sonic', 'Made By Me (Haxker_6666666)', {
    'Enable Sonic',
    'Disable Sonic',
}, function(p49)
    if p49 == 'Enable Sonic' then
        game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.FieldOfView = 120
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 150
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = 70
    elseif p49 == 'Disable Sonic' then
        game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.FieldOfView = 80
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.JumpPower = 50
    end
end)

_FEScripts:NewDropdown('FE Remove Animaton (Dont Walk Or Jump)', 'FE Remove Animaton', {
    'Enable FE Remove Animaton (Dont Walk Or Jump)',
    'Disable FE Remove Animaton (Dont Walk Or Jump)',
}, function(p53)
    if p53 == 'Enable FE Remove Animaton' then
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = true
    elseif p53 == 'Disable FE Remove Animaton (Dont Walk Or Jump)' then
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = false
    end
end)
_FEScripts:NewDropdown('FE Freeze Character', 'FE Freeze Character', {
    'Enable FE Freeze Character',
    'Disable FE Freeze Character',
}, function(p54)
    if p54 == 'Enable FE Freeze Character' then
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = true
    elseif p54 == 'Disable FE Freeze Character' then
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = false
    end
end)
_FEScripts:NewButton('FE Upside down', 'Op Script', function()
    local _Character = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character
    local _HumanoidRootPart = _Character:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart')
    local v57 = _HumanoidRootPart:Clone()

    _Character.Parent = nil
    _HumanoidRootPart.Parent = v57
    _HumanoidRootPart.RootJoint.Part0 = nil
    v57.Parent = _Character
    _Character.Parent = workspace

    local _Heartbeat = game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat

    _HumanoidRootPart.Transparency = 0.5

    while _Heartbeat:Wait() and (_Character and _Character.Parent) do
        _HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v57.CFrame
        _HumanoidRootPart.Orientation = _HumanoidRootPart.Orientation + Vector3.new(0, 0, 180)
        _HumanoidRootPart.Position = _HumanoidRootPart.Position - Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
        _HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = v57.Velocity
    end
end)
_FEScripts:NewButton('FE Wall Walk', 'Made By Me (Haxker_6666666)', function()
    loadstring(game:HttpGet('https://pastebin.com/raw/zXk4Rq2r'))()
end)
_FEScripts:NewButton('FE Headless ( Free )', 'Op Script', function()
    game.Players.LocalPlayer.ChildAdded:Connect(function()
        wait()
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.ChildRemoved:Connect(function()
            CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame

            print(CFrame)
        end)
    end)
    game.Players.LocalPlayer.ChildAdded:Connect(function()
        task.wait()

        y = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild('Humanoid')

        if y ~= nil then
            y:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead, false)
        end

        x = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild('Head')

        if x ~= nil then
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head:Destroy()
        end

        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame
    end)
    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead, false)
    wait()

    x = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild('Head')

    if x ~= nil then
        x:Destroy()
    end
end)

}, function(p66)
    if p66 == 'Enable FE Fake Lag' then
        FakeLag = true

        repeat
            wait()

            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = true

            wait(0.05)

            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = false

            wait(0.05)
        until FakeLag == false
    elseif p66 == 'Disable FE Fake Lag' then
        FakeLag = false
    end
end)

_FEScripts:NewButton('FE Chat Bot', 'Made By Me (Haxker_6666666)', function()
    local _HttpService2 = game:GetService('HttpService')
    local _Players2 = game:GetService('Players')

    game:GetService('UserInputService')

    local u77 = 'en'
    local u78 = 'True'

    local function u82(p79, p80)
        local v81 = _HttpService2:JSONDecode((game:HttpGet('https://api.simsimi.net/v2/?text=' .. p79 .. '&lc=' .. u77 .. '&cf=' .. u78)))

        wait()
        game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').DefaultChatSystemChatEvents.SayMessageRequest:FireServer(p80 .. ' ' .. v81.success, 'All')
    end

    _Players2.PlayerChatted:Connect(function(_, p83, p84)
        local v85, v86, v87 = pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())

        while true do
            local v88

            v87, v88 = v85(v86, v87)

            if v87 == nil then
                break
            end
            if (_Players2.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - v88.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).magnitude <= 10 and p83.Name == v88.Name then
                u82(p84, p83.Name)
            end
        end
    end)
end)

_Render:NewButton('Realistic Fog Spawner ( Tool ) ( Not FE )', 'Realistic Fog Spawner', function()
    local u282 = Color3.fromRGB(125, 125, 125)
    local u283 = 50
    local u284 = 0.5
    local _Tool = Instance.new('Tool')

    _Tool.Name = 'Fog Spawner'
    _Tool.RequiresHandle = false
    _Tool.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack

    local function u289(p286)
        local _Part = Instance.new('Part')

        _Part.Name = 'Fog'
        _Part.Size = Vector3.new(u283, u283, u283)
        _Part.Transparency = 1
        _Part.CanCollide = false
        _Part.Anchored = true
        _Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(p286)
        _Part.Parent = workspace

        local _ParticleEmitter = Instance.new('ParticleEmitter')

        _ParticleEmitter.Name = 'FogEmitter'
        _ParticleEmitter.Parent = _Part
        _ParticleEmitter.Enabled = true
        _ParticleEmitter.Rate = 100
        _ParticleEmitter.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(10, 15)
        _ParticleEmitter.Speed = NumberRange.new(1, 5)
        _ParticleEmitter.VelocitySpread = 180
        _ParticleEmitter.Rotation = NumberRange.new(0, 360)
        _ParticleEmitter.RotSpeed = NumberRange.new(-5, 5)
        _ParticleEmitter.Size = NumberSequence.new(u283)
        _ParticleEmitter.Transparency = NumberSequence.new(u284)
        _ParticleEmitter.Acceleration = Vector3.new(0, -5, 0)
        _ParticleEmitter.Color = ColorSequence.new(u282)
    end
    local function u290()
        if _Tool.Parent == game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character then
            u289(game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse().Hit.Position)
        end
    end

    _Tool.Equipped:Connect(function()
        game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse().Button1Down:Connect(u290)
    end)
    _Tool.Unequipped:Connect(function()
        game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse().Button1Down:Disconnect()
    end)
end)

}, function(p491)

        AntiFling = true

        local v492, v493, v494 = pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())

        local function u500(p495)
            if AntiFling and p495.Character then
                local v496, v497, v498 = pairs(p495.Character:GetDescendants())

                while true do
                    local v499

                    v498, v499 = v496(v497, v498)

                    if v498 == nil then
                        break

                    if v499:IsA('BasePart') and v499.CanCollide then
                        v499.CanCollide = false
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        while true do
            local u501

            v494, u501 = v492(v493, v494)

            if v494 == nil then
                break
            end
            if u501 ~= game.Players then
                game:GetService('RunService').Stepped:connect(function()
                    u500(u501)
                end)
            end
        end

        game.Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function()
            if v ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and antifling then
                game:GetService('RunService').Stepped:connect(function()
                    u500(v)
                end)
            end
        end)
    elseif p491 == 'Disable FE Anti Fling 2' then
        AntiFling = true

        local v502, v503, v504 = pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())

        while true do
            local v505

            v504, v505 = v502(v503, v504)

            if v504 == nil then
                break

_FlingScript:NewDropdown('Walk Fling', 'Walk Fling', {
    'Enable Walk Fling',
    'Disable Walk Fling',
}, function(p511)
    if p511 == 'Enable Walk Fling' then
        if game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage'):FindFirstChild('juisdfj0i32i0eidsuf0iok') then
            hiddenfling = true
        else
            hiddenfling = true
            detection = Instance.new('Decal')
            detection.Name = 'juisdfj0i32i0eidsuf0iok'
            detection.Parent = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');

            (function()
                local v512 = nil
                local v513 = nil
                local v514 = 0.1

                repeat
                    game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat:Wait()
                until hiddenfling

                local _LocalPlayer6 = game.Players.LocalPlayer

                if hiddenfling then
                    local _Velocity = v513.Velocity

                    v513.Velocity = _Velocity * 10000 + Vector3.new(0, 10000, 0)

                    game:GetService('RunService').RenderStepped:Wait()

                    if v512 and (v512.Parent and (v513 and v513.Parent)) then
                        v513.Velocity = _Velocity
                    end

                    game:GetService('RunService').Stepped:Wait()

                    if v512 and (v512.Parent and (v513 and v513.Parent)) then
                        v513.Velocity = _Velocity + Vector3.new(0, v514, 0)
                        v514 = v514 * -1
                    end
                end

                game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat:Wait()

                v512 = _LocalPlayer6.Character
                v513 = v512:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart') or (v512:FindFirstChild('Torso') or v512:FindFirstChild('UpperTorso'))

                if hiddenfling and not (v512 and (v512.Parent and (v513 and v513.Parent))) then
                else
                end
            end)()
        end
    elseif p511 == 'Disable Walk Fling' then
        AntiFling = true
        hiddenfling = false
    end
end)

local _MurderMystery2 = _Games:NewSection('Murder Mystery 2')

_MurderMystery2:NewButton('Unlock All Weapons', 'This Script Only Works In Murder Mystery 2', function()
    local _Database = getrenv()._G.Database
    local _PlayerData = getrenv()._G.PlayerData
    local v542 = next
    local _Item = _Database.Item
    local v544 = nil
    local v545 = {
        min = 1,
        max = 5,
    }
    local u546 = {}

    while true do
        local v547

        v544, v547 = v542(_Item, v544)

        if v544 == nil then
            break
        end

        u546[v544] = math.random(v545.min, v545.max)
    end

    local _Weapons = _PlayerData.Weapons

    game:GetService('RunService'):BindToRenderStep('InventoryUpdate', 0, function()
        _Weapons.Owned = u546
    end)

    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health = 0
end)

_Games:NewSection('Strongest Battleground'):NewButton('Strongest Battleground Script', 'This Script Hub Only Works In Strongest Battleground Script', function()
    game.StarterGui:SetCore('SendNotification', {
        Title = 'Strongest Battleground Script Loaded',
        Text = 'Made by Haxker_6666666',
        Icon = '',
        Duration = 20,
    })

    function isNumber(p555)
        if tonumber(p555) ~= nil or p555 == 'inf' then
            return true
        end
    end

    local v556 = 3
    local _Heartbeat2 = game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat
    local v558 = true
    local _Character7 = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character
    local v560

    if _Character7 then
        v560 = _Character7:FindFirstChildWhichIsA('Humanoid')
    else
        v560 = _Character7
    end

    while v558 and (_Heartbeat2:Wait() and (_Character7 and (v560 and v560.Parent))) do
        if v560.MoveDirection.Magnitude > 0 then
            if v556 and isNumber(v556) then
                _Character7:TranslateBy(v560.MoveDirection * tonumber(v556))
            else
                _Character7:TranslateBy(v560.MoveDirection)
            end
        end
    end
end)

    local v563, v564, v565 = pairs(game.CoreGui:GetDescendants())

    while true do
        local v566

        if v565 == nil then

_Settings:NewDropdown('Set FPS Cap', 'Sets The FPS Cap', {
    '60 FPS ( Original FPS )',
    '120 FPS',
    'Max FPS',
}, function(p567)
    if p567 == '60 FPS ( Original FPS )' then
        setfpscap(60)
    elseif p567 == '120 FPS' then
        setfpscap(120)
    elseif p567 == 'Max FPS' then
        setfpscap(1000)
    end
end)
_Settings:NewDropdown('Hide/Show Toggle Button', 'Hide/Show The Toggle Button', {
    'Hide',
    'Show',
}, function(p568)
    if p568 == 'Hide' then
        _ImageButton.Visible = false
    elseif p568 == 'Show' then
        _ImageButton.Visible = true
    end
end)
_Settings:NewDropdown('Change Toggle Button Shape', 'Changes The Toggle Button Shapes', {
    'Squircle ( Original Shape )',
    'Circle',
    'Rectangle',
}, function(p569)
    if p569 == 'Squircle ( Original Shape )' then
        _UICorner2.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 12)
        _UICorner2.Parent = _ImageButton
    elseif p569 == 'Circle' then
        _UICorner2.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 219)
        _UICorner2.Parent = _ImageButton
    elseif p569 == 'Rectangle' then
        _UICorner2.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 0)
        _UICorner2.Parent = _ImageButton
    end
end)
_Settings:NewDropdown('Change Toggle Button Color', 'Changes The Toggle Button Color', {
    'Purple Blue ( Original Color )',
    'Green',
    'Dark Green',
}, function(p570)
    if p570 == 'Purple Blue ( Original Color )' then
        _UIStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(86, 76, 251)
        _UIStroke.Parent = _ImageButton
    elseif p570 == 'Green' then
        _UIStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(55, 219, 70)
        _UIStroke.Parent = _ImageButton
    elseif p570 == 'Dark Green' then
        _UIStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(84, 125, 60)
        _UIStroke.Parent = _ImageButton
    end
end)
_Settings:NewDropdown('Change Toggle Button Size', 'Changes The Toggle Button Size', {
    'Medium ( Original Size )',
    'Small',
    'Large',
}, function(p571)
    if p571 == 'Medium ( Original Size )' then
        _ImageButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, 47, 0, 47)
